<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">Religion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Religion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kharkov002.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Kharkov002.jpg/150px-Kharkov002.jpg" width="150" height="261" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Kharkov002.jpg/225px-Kharkov002.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Kharkov002.jpg/300px-Kharkov002.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1276" data-file-height="2218" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kharkov002.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The <a href="/wiki/Annunciation_Cathedral,_Kharkiv" title="Annunciation Cathedral, Kharkiv">St. Annunciation Orthodox Cathedral</a> is one of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_tallest_Orthodox_churches" class="mw-redirect" title="List of tallest Orthodox churches">tallest Orthodox churches</a> in the world, which was built in Kharkiv on October 2, 1888.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Kharkiv is an important religious center in Eastern Ukraine.</p>
<p>There are many old and new cathedrals, associated with various churches in Kharkiv.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Assumption_Cathedral,_Kharkiv" class="mw-redirect" title="Assumption Cathedral, Kharkiv">St. Assumption Orthodox Cathedral</a> was built in Kharkiv in the 1680s and re-built in 1820s-1830s.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov-92">[91]</a></sup></p>
<p>The St. Pokrovsky Orthodox Monastery Cathedral was created in Kharkiv in 1689–1729.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov2_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov2-93">[92]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-pokrovsky-monastyr_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pokrovsky-monastyr-94">[93]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Annunciation_Cathedral,_Kharkiv" title="Annunciation Cathedral, Kharkiv">St. Annunciation Orthodox Cathedral</a> is one of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_tallest_Orthodox_churches" class="mw-redirect" title="List of tallest Orthodox churches">tallest Orthodox churches</a> in the world. It was completed in Kharkiv on October 2, 1888.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov3_95-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov3-95">[94]</a></sup></p>
<p>The St. Trinity Orthodox Cathedral was built in Kharkiv in 1758–1764 and re-built in 1857–1861.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov4_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov4-96">[95]</a></sup></p>
<p>The St. Valentine Orthodox Cathedral was built in Kharkiv in the 2010s.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov5_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov5-97">[96]</a></sup></p>
<p>The St. Tamara Orthodox Cathedral was built in Kharkiv in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov6_98-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov6-98">[97]</a></sup></p>
<p>The St. Peace Bringing Wives Orthodox Cathedral was built in green park near <a href="/wiki/Zerkal%CA%B9naya_struya" title="Zerkalʹnaya struya">Mirror Stream</a> fountain in August, 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov7_99-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov7-99">[98]</a></sup></p>
<p>The Roman Catholic St. Mary Cathedral was built in Kharkiv in 1887–1892.</p>
<p>There is the old <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Choral_Synagogue" title="Kharkiv Choral Synagogue">Kharkiv Choral Synagogue</a>, which was fully renovated in Kharkiv in 1991–2016. The Jewish population is around 8000 people in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-jewishkharkov_100-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-jewishkharkov-100">[99]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">Economy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Economy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The 2016–2020 economic development strategy: "Kharkiv Success Strategy", is created in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov8_101-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov8-101">[100]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kharkov9_102-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov9-102">[101]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kharkov10_103-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov10-103">[102]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="International_Economic_Forum">International Economic Forum</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: International Economic Forum">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The International Economic Forum: Innovations. Investments. Kharkiv Innitiatives! is being conducted in Kharkiv every year.<sup id="cite_ref-led.org.ua_104-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-led.org.ua-104">[103]</a></sup></p>
<p>In 2015, the International Economic Forum: Innovations. Investments. Kharkiv Innitiatives! was attended by the diplomatic corps representatives from 17 world countries, working in Ukraine together with top-management of trans-national corporations and investment funds; plus Ukrainian People’s Deputies; plus Ukrainian Central government officials, who determine the national economic development strategy; plus local government managers, who perform practical steps in implementing that strategy; plus managers of technical assistance to Ukraine; plus business and NGO’s representatives; plus media people.<sup id="cite_ref-led.org.ua_104-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-led.org.ua-104">[103]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-usa.mfa.gov.ua_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-usa.mfa.gov.ua-105">[104]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kmu.gov.ua_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kmu.gov.ua-106">[105]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ukraine.usembassy.gov_107-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ukraine.usembassy.gov-107">[106]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-usembassykyiv.wordpress.com_108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-usembassykyiv.wordpress.com-108">[107]</a></sup></p>
<p>The key topics of the plenary sessions and panel discussions of the International Economic Forum: Innovations. Investments. Kharkiv Innitiatives! are the implementation of Strategy for Sustainable Development “Ukraine – 2020”, the results achieved and plan of further actions to reform the local government and territorial organization of power in Ukraine, export promotion and attraction of investments in Ukraine, new opportunities for public-private partnerships, practical steps to create “electronic government”, issues of energy conservation and development of oil and gas industry in the Kharkiv Region, creating an effective system of production and processing of agricultural products, investment projects that will receive funding from the State Fund for Regional Development, development of international integration, preparation for privatization of state enterprises.<sup id="cite_ref-led.org.ua_104-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-led.org.ua-104">[103]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-usa.mfa.gov.ua_105-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-usa.mfa.gov.ua-105">[104]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kmu.gov.ua_106-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kmu.gov.ua-106">[105]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ukraine.usembassy.gov_107-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ukraine.usembassy.gov-107">[106]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-usembassykyiv.wordpress.com_108-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-usembassykyiv.wordpress.com-108">[107]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="International_Industrial_Exhibitions">International Industrial Exhibitions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: International Industrial Exhibitions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The international industrial exhibitions are usually conducted at the Radmir Expohall exhibition center in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-radmir-expohall_109-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-radmir-expohall-109">[108]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Industrial_corporations">Industrial corporations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Industrial corporations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>During the Soviet era, Kharkiv was the capital of industrial production in Ukraine and the third largest<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>centre of industry and commerce in the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">USSR</a>. After the <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Soviet_Union_(1985%E2%80%931991)#Dissolution_of_the_USSR" class="mw-redirect" title="History of the Soviet Union (1985–1991)">collapse of the Soviet Union</a> the largely defence-systems-oriented industrial production of the city decreased significantly. In the early 2000s, the industry started to recover and adapt to market economy needs. Now there are more than 380&#160;industrial enterprises concentrated in the city, which have a total number of 150,000 employees.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> The enterprises form machine-building, electro-technology, instrument-making, and energy conglomerates.</p>
<p>State-owned industrial giants, such as <a href="/wiki/Turboatom" title="Turboatom">Turboatom</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Elektrotyazhmash&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Elektrotyazhmash (page does not exist)">Elektrotyazhmash</a><sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">[109]</a></sup> occupy 17% of the heavy power equipment construction (e.g., turbines) market worldwide. Multipurpose aircraft are produced by the <a href="/wiki/Antonov" title="Antonov">Antonov</a> aircraft manufacturing plant. The <a href="/wiki/Malyshev_factory" class="mw-redirect" title="Malyshev factory">Malyshev factory</a> produces not only <a href="/wiki/Armoured_fighting_vehicle" title="Armoured fighting vehicle">armoured fighting vehicles</a>, but also harvesters. <a href="/wiki/Khartron" title="Khartron">Khartron</a><sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">[110]</a></sup> is the leading designer of space and commercial control systems in Ukraine and the former <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Independent_States" title="Commonwealth of Independent States">CIS</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="IT_industry">IT industry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: IT industry">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The IT industry is represented by a few hundred small IT <a href="/wiki/Startup_company" title="Startup company">start ups</a>, which form a cluster of IT companies in Kharkiv<sup id="cite_ref-economist.com_112-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-economist.com-112">[111]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-it-kharkiv_113-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-it-kharkiv-113">[112]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kharkivglobal_114-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkivglobal-114">[113]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-triolan_115-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-triolan-115">[114]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Finance_industry">Finance industry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Finance industry">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kharkiv is also the headquarters of one of the largest Ukrainian banks, <a href="/wiki/UkrSibbank" title="UkrSibbank">UkrSibbank</a>, which has been part of the <a href="/wiki/BNP_Paribas" title="BNP Paribas">BNP Paribas</a> group since December 2005.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Trade_industry">Trade industry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Trade industry">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>There are many large modern shopping malls in Kharkiv.</p>
<p>There are a large number of markets:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Barabashovo_market&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Barabashovo market (page does not exist)">Barabashovo market</a> is the largest market in Ukraine and one of the largest markets in Europe.</li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Blagoveshinskiy&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Blagoveshinskiy (page does not exist)">Blagoveshinskiy</a> market.</li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Konniy&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Konniy (page does not exist)">Konniy</a> "horse" market.</li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Sumskoi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sumskoi (page does not exist)">Sumskoi</a> market <sup id="cite_ref-kharkov11_116-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov11-116">[115]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Raiskiy&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Raiskiy (page does not exist)">Raiskiy</a> book market.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Science_and_education">Science and education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Science and education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tmulti tright">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Higher_education">Higher education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Higher education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_National_University" class="mw-redirect" title="Kharkiv National University">Vasyl N. Karazin Kharkiv National University</a> is the most prestigious reputable classic university, which was founded due to the efforts by <a href="/wiki/Vasily_Karazin" title="Vasily Karazin">Vasily Karazin</a> in Kharkiv in 1804–1805.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov12_117-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov12-117">[116]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kiev_118-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kiev-118">[117]</a></sup> On 29 January&#160;[<a href="/wiki/Old_Style_and_New_Style_dates" title="Old Style and New Style dates">O.S.</a> 17 January]&#160;1805, the Decree on the Opening of the Imperial University in Kharkiv came into force.</p>
<p>The Roentgen Institute opened in 1931. It was a specialist cancer treatment facility with 87 research workers, 20 professors, and specialist medical staff. The facilities included chemical, physiology, and bacteriology experimental treatment laboratories. It produced x-ray apparatus for the whole country.<sup id="cite_ref-Socialist_Health_Association_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Socialist_Health_Association-33">[32]</a></sup></p>
<p>The city has 13&#160;national universities and numerous professional, technical and private higher education institutions, offering its students a wide range of disciplines. <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_National_University" class="mw-redirect" title="Kharkiv National University">Kharkiv National University</a> (12,000&#160;students), <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Polytechnical_Institute" class="mw-redirect" title="Kharkiv Polytechnical Institute">National Technical University "KhPI"</a> (20,000&#160;students), <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_National_University_of_Radioelectronics" title="Kharkiv National University of Radioelectronics">Kharkiv National University of Radioelectronics</a> (12,000&#160;students), <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_National_Aerospace_University_%22KhAI%22" class="mw-redirect" title="Kharkiv National Aerospace University &quot;KhAI&quot;">Kharkiv National Aerospace University "KhAI"</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ukrainian_Academy_of_Pharmacy&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ukrainian Academy of Pharmacy (page does not exist)">Kharkiv National University of Pharmacy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_National_Medical_University" title="Kharkiv National Medical University">Kharkiv National Medical University</a> are the leading<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> universities in Ukraine.</p>
<p>More than 17,000&#160;faculty and research staff are employed in the institutions of higher education in Kharkiv.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Scientific_research">Scientific research</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Scientific research">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The city has a high concentration of research institutions, which are independent or loosely connected with the universities. Among them are three national science centres: <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Institute_of_Physics_and_Technology" title="Kharkiv Institute of Physics and Technology">Kharkiv Institute of Physics and Technology</a>, Institute of Meteorology, Institute for Experimental and Clinical Veterinary Medicine and 20&#160;national research institutions of the <a href="/wiki/National_Academy_of_Science_of_Ukraine" class="mw-redirect" title="National Academy of Science of Ukraine">National Academy of Science of Ukraine</a>, such as the <a href="/wiki/B_Verkin_Institute_for_Low_Temperature_Physics_and_Engineering" class="mw-redirect" title="B Verkin Institute for Low Temperature Physics and Engineering">B Verkin Institute for Low Temperature Physics and Engineering</a>, <a href="/wiki/Institute_for_Problems_of_Cryobiology_and_Cryomedicine" class="mw-redirect" title="Institute for Problems of Cryobiology and Cryomedicine">Institute for Problems of Cryobiology and Cryomedicine</a>, State Scientific Institution "Institute for Single Crystals", Usikov Institute of Radiophysics and Electronics (IRE), Institute of Radio Astronomy (IRA), and others. A total number of 26,000&#160;scientists are working in research and development.</p>
<p>A number of world-renowned scientific schools appeared in Kharkiv, such as the <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Theoretical_Physics_School" title="Kharkiv Theoretical Physics School">theoretical physics school</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Mathematical_School" title="Kharkiv Mathematical School">mathematical school</a>.</p>
<p>There is the Kharkiv Scientists House in the city, which was built by A. N. Beketov, architect in Kharkiv in 1900. All the scientists like to meet and discuss various scientific topics at the Kharkiv Scientists House in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-khdu_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-khdu-119">[118]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Public_libraries">Public libraries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Public libraries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In addition to the libraries affiliated with the various universities and research institutions, the Kharkiv State Scientific V. Korolenko-library is a major research library.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Secondary_schools">Secondary schools</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Secondary schools">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kharkiv has 212 (<a href="/wiki/Secondary_education" title="Secondary education">secondary education</a>) schools, including 10 <a href="/wiki/Lyceum" title="Lyceum">lyceums</a> and 20&#160;<a href="/wiki/Gymnasium_(school)" title="Gymnasium (school)">gymnasiums</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Education_centers">Education centers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Education centers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>There is the educational "Landau Center", which is named after Prof. L.D. Landau, Nobel laureate in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-landaucentre_120-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-landaucentre-120">[119]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">Culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kharkiv is one of the main cultural centres in Ukraine. It is home to 20 museums, over 10 theaters and a number of art galleries. Large music and cinema festivals are hosted in Kharkiv almost every year.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Theaters">Theaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Theaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Kharkiv National Academic Opera and Ballet Theater named after N. V. Lysenko is a biggest theater in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-hatob_121-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hatob-121">[120]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-hatob2_122-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hatob2-122">[121]</a></sup></p>
<p>The Kharkiv State Academic Drama Theater named after T. G. Shevchenko is popular among Ukrainian speaking people <sup id="cite_ref-theatre-shevchenko_123-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-theatre-shevchenko-123">[122]</a></sup></p>
<p>The Kharkiv Academic Russian Drama Theater named after A.S. Pushkin was recently renovated, and it is quite popular among the locals.<sup id="cite_ref-rusdrama_124-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rusdrama-124">[123]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Literature">Literature</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Literature">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the 1930s Kharkiv was referred to as a Literary <a href="/wiki/Klondike_Gold_Rush" title="Klondike Gold Rush">Klondike</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2012)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> It was the centre for the work of literary luminaries such as: <a href="/wiki/Les_Kurbas" title="Les Kurbas">Les Kurbas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mykola_Kulish" title="Mykola Kulish">Mykola Kulish</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mykola_Khvylovy" title="Mykola Khvylovy">Mykola Khvylovy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mykola_Zerov" title="Mykola Zerov">Mykola Zerov</a>, <a href="/wiki/Valerian_Pidmohylny" title="Valerian Pidmohylny">Valerian Pidmohylny</a>, Pavlo Filipovych, Marko Voronny, Oleksa Slisarenko. Over 100 of these writers were repressed during the Stalinist purges of the 1930s. This tragic event in Ukrainian history is called the "Executed Renaissance" (Rozstrilene vidrodzhennia). Today a literary museum located on Frunze Street marks their work and achievements.</p>
<p>Today, Kharkiv is often referred to as the "capital city" of Ukrainian <a href="/wiki/Science_fiction" title="Science fiction">Science fiction</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fantasy" title="Fantasy">Fantasy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">[124]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">[125]</a></sup> It is the home to a number of popular writers, such as <a href="/wiki/H._L._Oldie" title="H. L. Oldie">H. L. Oldie</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Zorich" title="Alexander Zorich">Alexander Zorich</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andrey_Dashkov" title="Andrey Dashkov">Andrey Dashkov</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yuri_Nikitin_(author)" title="Yuri Nikitin (author)">Yuri Nikitin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andrey_Valentinov" title="Andrey Valentinov">Andrey Valentinov</a>; most of them <a href="/wiki/Russian_language_in_Ukraine" title="Russian language in Ukraine">write in Russian</a> and are popular in both Russia and Ukraine. The annual <a href="/wiki/Science_fiction_convention" title="Science fiction convention">science fiction convention</a> "Star Bridge" (Звёздный мост) has been held in Kharkiv since 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">[126]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Music">Music</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Music">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>There is the <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Philharmonic_Society" title="Kharkiv Philharmonic Society">Kharkiv Philharmonic Society</a> in the city.</p>
<p>There is the Organ Music Hall in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-filarmonia3_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-filarmonia3-128">[127]</a></sup> The Organ Music Hall is situated at the <a href="/wiki/Dormition_Cathedral,_Kharkiv" title="Dormition Cathedral, Kharkiv">Assumption Cathedral</a> presently. The <a href="/wiki/Rieger%E2%80%93Kloss" title="Rieger–Kloss">Rieger–Kloss</a> organ was installed in the building of the Organ Music Hall back in 1986. The new Organ Music Hall will be opened at the extensively renovated building of <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Philharmonic_Society" title="Kharkiv Philharmonic Society">Kharkiv Philharmonic Society</a> in Kharkiv in November, 2016.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Conservatory" class="mw-redirect" title="Kharkiv Conservatory">Kharkiv Conservatory</a> is in the city.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_National_Kotlyarevsky_University_of_Arts" title="Kharkiv National Kotlyarevsky University of Arts">Kharkiv National University of Arts named after I.P. Kotlyarevsky</a> is situated in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov13_129-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov13-129">[128]</a></sup></p>
<p>Kharkiv sponsors the prestigious <a href="/wiki/Hnat_Khotkevych" title="Hnat Khotkevych">Hnat Khotkevych</a> International Music Competition of Performers of Ukrainian Folk Instruments, which takes place every three years. Since 1997 four tri-annual competitions have taken place. The 2010 competition was cancelled by the Ukrainian Ministry of Culture two days before its opening.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">[129]</a></sup></p>
<p>The music festival: "Kharkiv - City of Kind Hopes" is conducted in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-filarmonia4_131-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-filarmonia4-131">[130]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Movies_festival">Movies festival</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Movies festival">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The "Kharkiv Lilacs" international movie festival is very popular among the movie stars, makers, producers in Ukraine, Eastern Europe, Western Europe and North America.<sup id="cite_ref-sirenfest.net.ua_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sirenfest.net.ua-132">[131]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-times.kh.ua_133-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-times.kh.ua-133">[132]</a></sup></p>
<p>The festival is usually conducted in May every year.<sup id="cite_ref-sirenfest.net.ua_132-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sirenfest.net.ua-132">[131]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-sirenfest.net.ua_132-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sirenfest.net.ua-132">[131]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-times.kh.ua_133-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-times.kh.ua-133">[132]</a></sup></p>
<p>There is a special alley with the metal hand prints by the popular movies actors at Shevchenko park in Kharkiv. <sup id="cite_ref-times.kh.ua_133-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-times.kh.ua-133">[132]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-dozor_134-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dozor-134">[133]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Visual_arts">Visual arts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Visual arts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kharkiv was/is a home for many famous painters <a href="/wiki/Ilya_Repin" title="Ilya Repin">Ilya Repin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zinaida_Serebryakova" class="mw-redirect" title="Zinaida Serebryakova">Zinaida Serebryakova</a>, <a href="/wiki/Henryk_Siemiradzki" title="Henryk Siemiradzki">Henryk Siemiradzki</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vasyl_Yermilov" class="mw-redirect" title="Vasyl Yermilov">Vasyl Yermilov</a>,<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> etc. There are many modern arts galleries in the city. For example: the Yermilov Centre, Lilacs Gallery, the Kharkiv Art Museum, the Kharkiv Municipal Gallery, the AC Gallery, Palladium Gallery, fthe Semiradsky Gallery, AVEK Gallery, and Arts of Slobozhanshyna Gallery.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Museums">Museums</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Museums">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>There is the Kharkiv History Museum named after M. F. Sumtsov in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-museum_135-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-museum-135">[134]</a></sup></p>
<p>The Natural History Museum at V. N. Karazin Kharkiv National University was founded in Kharkiv on April 2, 1807. The museum is visited by 40000 visitors every year.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov14_136-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov14-136">[135]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kiev2_137-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kiev2-137">[136]</a></sup></p>
<p>The V. N. Karazin Kharkiv National University History Museum was established in Kharkiv in 1972.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov15_138-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov15-138">[137]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kharkov16_139-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov16-139">[138]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kiev3_140-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kiev3-140">[139]</a></sup></p>
<p>The V. N. Karazin Kharkiv National University Archeology Museum was founded in Kharkiv on March 20, 1998. <sup id="cite_ref-maesu_141-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-maesu-141">[140]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kiev4_142-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kiev4-142">[141]</a></sup></p>
<p>The National Technical University "Kharkiv Polytechnical Institute" Museum was created in Kharkiv on December 29, 1972.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkov17_143-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov17-143">[142]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kharkov18_144-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov18-144">[143]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kharkov19_145-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov19-145">[144]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kharkov20_146-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov20-146">[145]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kiev5_147-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kiev5-147">[146]</a></sup></p>
<p>The National Aerospace University "Kharkiv Aviation Institute" Museum was founded on May 29, 1992.<sup id="cite_ref-kiev6_148-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kiev6-148">[147]</a></sup></p>
<p>The "National University of Pharmacy" Museum was founded in Kharkiv on September 15, 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-nuph_149-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nuph-149">[148]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-nuph2_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nuph2-150">[149]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kiev7_151-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kiev7-151">[150]</a></sup></p>
<p>There are around 147 museums in the Kharkiv's region.<sup id="cite_ref-museums_152-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-museums-152">[151]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Landmarks">Landmarks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Landmarks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:%D0%A4%D0%B5%D0%B9%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/%D0%A4%D0%B5%D0%B9%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA.jpg/150px-%D0%A4%D0%B5%D0%B9%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA.jpg" width="150" height="100" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/%D0%A4%D0%B5%D0%B9%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA.jpg/225px-%D0%A4%D0%B5%D0%B9%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/%D0%A4%D0%B5%D0%B9%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA.jpg/300px-%D0%A4%D0%B5%D0%B9%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA.jpg 2x" data-file-width="448" data-file-height="298" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:%D0%A4%D0%B5%D0%B9%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
National holiday's fireworks on <a href="/wiki/Freedom_Square,_Kharkiv" class="mw-redirect" title="Freedom Square, Kharkiv">Freedom Square</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Of the many attractions of the Kharkiv city are the: <a href="/wiki/Assumption_Cathedral,_Kharkiv" class="mw-redirect" title="Assumption Cathedral, Kharkiv">Dormition Cathedral</a>, <a href="/wiki/Annunciation_Cathedral,_Kharkiv" title="Annunciation Cathedral, Kharkiv">Annunciation Cathedral</a>, <a href="/wiki/Derzhprom" title="Derzhprom">Derzhprom</a> building, <a href="/wiki/Freedom_Square,_Kharkiv" class="mw-redirect" title="Freedom Square, Kharkiv">Freedom Square</a>, <a href="/wiki/Taras_Shevchenko" title="Taras Shevchenko">Taras Shevchenko</a> Monument, Mirror Stream, Historical Museum, <a href="/wiki/Kharkov_Choral_Synagogue" class="mw-redirect" title="Kharkov Choral Synagogue">Choral Synagogue</a>, T.&#160;Shevchenko Gardens, Zoo, Children's narrow-gauge railroad, World War I Tank Mk V, Memorial Complex, and many more.</p>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/2014_Russian_annexation_of_Crimea" class="mw-redirect" title="2014 Russian annexation of Crimea">2014 Russian annexation of Crimea</a> the monument to <a href="/wiki/Petro_Konashevych-Sahaidachny" title="Petro Konashevych-Sahaidachny">Petro Konashevych-Sahaidachny</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">Sevastopol</a> was removed and handed over to Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">[152]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sport">Sport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Sport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:(79)_BYCICLE_COMPETITION_AT_BYCICLE_DAY_IN_CITY_OF_KHARKIV_STATE_OF_UKRAINE_PHOTOGRAPH_BY_VIKTOR_O_LEDENYOV_20160709.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/%2879%29_BYCICLE_COMPETITION_AT_BYCICLE_DAY_IN_CITY_OF_KHARKIV_STATE_OF_UKRAINE_PHOTOGRAPH_BY_VIKTOR_O_LEDENYOV_20160709.jpg/150px-%2879%29_BYCICLE_COMPETITION_AT_BYCICLE_DAY_IN_CITY_OF_KHARKIV_STATE_OF_UKRAINE_PHOTOGRAPH_BY_VIKTOR_O_LEDENYOV_20160709.jpg" width="150" height="250" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/%2879%29_BYCICLE_COMPETITION_AT_BYCICLE_DAY_IN_CITY_OF_KHARKIV_STATE_OF_UKRAINE_PHOTOGRAPH_BY_VIKTOR_O_LEDENYOV_20160709.jpg/225px-%2879%29_BYCICLE_COMPETITION_AT_BYCICLE_DAY_IN_CITY_OF_KHARKIV_STATE_OF_UKRAINE_PHOTOGRAPH_BY_VIKTOR_O_LEDENYOV_20160709.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/%2879%29_BYCICLE_COMPETITION_AT_BYCICLE_DAY_IN_CITY_OF_KHARKIV_STATE_OF_UKRAINE_PHOTOGRAPH_BY_VIKTOR_O_LEDENYOV_20160709.jpg/300px-%2879%29_BYCICLE_COMPETITION_AT_BYCICLE_DAY_IN_CITY_OF_KHARKIV_STATE_OF_UKRAINE_PHOTOGRAPH_BY_VIKTOR_O_LEDENYOV_20160709.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1536" data-file-height="2560" /></a>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kharkiv_International_Marathon">Kharkiv International Marathon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Kharkiv International Marathon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Kharkiv International Marathon is considered as a prime international sportive event, attracting many thousands of professional sportsmen, young people, students, professors, locals and tourists to travel to Kharkiv and to participate in the international event.<sup id="cite_ref-kharkivmarathon_155-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkivmarathon-155">[154]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-marathonrunnersdiary_156-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-marathonrunnersdiary-156">[155]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-sportevent_157-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sportevent-157">[156]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kharkov21_158-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kharkov21-158">[157]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span id="Football_(soccer)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Football_.28soccer.29">Football (soccer)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Football (soccer)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The most popular sport is <a href="/wiki/Football_(soccer)" class="mw-redirect" title="Football (soccer)">football</a>. The city has several football clubs playing in the Ukrainian National competitions. The most successful is <i><a href="/wiki/FC_Dynamo_Kharkiv" title="FC Dynamo Kharkiv">FC Dynamo Kharkiv</a></i> that won eight national titles back in 1920s-1930s.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/FC_Metalist_1925_Kharkiv" title="FC Metalist 1925 Kharkiv">FC Metalist 1925 Kharkiv</a>, which plays at the <a href="/wiki/Metalist_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Metalist Stadium">Metalist Stadium</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/FC_Helios" class="mw-redirect" title="FC Helios">FC Helios</a>, which plays at the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Arsenal-Bavariya_Stadium&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Arsenal-Bavariya Stadium (page does not exist)">Helios Arena</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/FC_Arsenal_Kharkiv" title="FC Arsenal Kharkiv">FC Arsenal Kharkiv</a>, which plays at the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Arsenal-Spartak_Stadium&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Arsenal-Spartak Stadium (page does not exist)">Arsenal-Spartak Stadium</a> (participates in regional competitions)</li>
</ul>
<p>There is also a female football club <a href="/wiki/WFC_Zhytlobud-1_Kharkiv" title="WFC Zhytlobud-1 Kharkiv">WFC Zhytlobud-1 Kharkiv</a>, which represented Ukraine in the European competitions and constantly is the main contender for the national title.</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Metalist_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Metalist Stadium">Metalist Stadium</a> hosted three group matches at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_sports">Other sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Other sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kharkiv also has an <a href="/wiki/Ice_hockey" title="Ice hockey">Ice Hockey</a> club, HC Vityaz Kharkiv who compete in the Ukrainian Vyscha Liga.</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Avangard_Budy" title="Avangard Budy">Avangard Budy</a> is a <a href="/wiki/Bandy" title="Bandy">bandy</a> club from Kharkiv, which won the Ukrainian championship in 2013.</p>
<p>There is a men's volleyball team <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lokomotiv_Kharkiv_Volleyball&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Lokomotiv Kharkiv Volleyball (page does not exist)">Lokomotiv Kharkiv</a> which performs in Ukraine and in the European competitions.</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/RC_Olymp" title="RC Olymp">RC Olimp'</a> is the city's <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">rugby union</a> club. They provide many players for the <a href="/wiki/Ukraine_national_rugby_union_team" title="Ukraine national rugby union team">national team</a>.</p>
<p>Tennis is a very popular sport in Kharkiv. There are many professional tennis courts in the city. <a href="/wiki/Elina_Svitolina" title="Elina Svitolina">Elina Svitolina</a> is a tennis player from Kharkiv.</p>
<p>There is a golf club in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-superiorresort_159-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-superiorresort-159">[158]</a></sup></p>
<p>Horseriding as a sport is very popular among the locals.<sup id="cite_ref-zabytki_160-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-zabytki-160">[159]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ippodrom_161-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ippodrom-161">[160]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ippodrom2_162-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ippodrom2-162">[161]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-konezavod_163-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-konezavod-163">[162]</a></sup> There are large stable and the horse riding facilities at Feldman Ecopark in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-feldman-ecopark_164-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-feldman-ecopark-164">[163]</a></sup></p>
<p>There is a growing interest to the cycling among the locals.<sup id="cite_ref-vesti-ukr_165-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vesti-ukr-165">[164]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-nezabarom_166-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nezabarom-166">[165]</a></sup> There is a large bicycles producing plant in Kharkiv.<sup id="cite_ref-usi_167-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-usi-167">[166]</a></sup> Presently, the modern bicycle highway is under the construction at "Leso park" district in Kharkiv.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sister_cities">Sister cities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Sister cities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_twin_towns_and_sister_cities_in_Ukraine" title="List of twin towns and sister cities in Ukraine">List of twin towns and sister cities in Ukraine</a></div>
<p>Kharkiv is <a href="/wiki/Twin_towns_and_sister_cities" class="mw-redirect" title="Twin towns and sister cities">twinned</a> with:<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">[167]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nobel_and_Fields_prize_winners">Nobel and Fields prize winners</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Nobel and Fields prize winners">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lev_Landau" title="Lev Landau">Lev Landau</a> – (originally from Baku) a head of the department of theoretical physics at the <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Institute_of_Physics_and_Technology" title="Kharkiv Institute of Physics and Technology">Kharkiv Institute of Physics and Technology</a>, a head of the department of experimental physics and a lecturer at the department of theoretical physics at the <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_State_University" class="mw-redirect" title="Kharkiv State University">Kharkiv State University</a>, a head of the department of theoretical physics at the at <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Polytechnic_Institute" title="Kharkiv Polytechnic Institute">Kharkiv Polytechnic Institute</a> 1932–37, Nobel Prize for Physics 1962</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Simon_Kuznets" title="Simon Kuznets">Simon Kuznets</a> (economics)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ilya_Ilyich_Mechnikov" class="mw-redirect" title="Ilya Ilyich Mechnikov">Ilya Mechnikov</a> (medicine)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Drinfeld" title="Vladimir Drinfeld">Vladimir Drinfeld</a> (mathematics)</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_people">Notable people</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Notable people">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The following people have been born or have lived in Kharkiv:</p>
<div>
<table class="multicol" role="presentation" style="border-collapse: collapse; padding: 0; border: 0; background:transparent; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td style="width:50%; text-align:left; vertical-align:top;">
<ul>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Boris_Amromin&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Boris Amromin (page does not exist)">Boris Amromin</a> — Israeli ice hockey player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nikolai_P._Barabashov" title="Nikolai P. Barabashov">Nikolai P. Barabashov</a> — astronomer, co-author of the first pictures of the far side of the moon</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pavel_Batitsky" title="Pavel Batitsky">Pavel Batitsky</a> — executed <a href="/wiki/Lavrentiy_Beria" title="Lavrentiy Beria">Lavrentiy Beria</a> after Khrushchevs' coup d'état in 1953, and commander-in-chief of the Soviet Air Defense Forces from 1966 to 1978</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Bobri" title="Vladimir Bobri">Vladimir Bobri</a> — illustrator, author, composer, educator and guitar historian</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Inna_Bohoslovska" title="Inna Bohoslovska">Inna Bohoslovska</a> — lawyer, politician and leader of the Ukrainian public organization <a href="/wiki/Viche" title="Viche">Viche</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sergei_Bortkiewicz" title="Sergei Bortkiewicz">Sergei Bortkiewicz</a> — Russian <a href="/wiki/Romantic_music" title="Romantic music">Romantic</a> <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pianist" title="Pianist">pianist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Maria_Burmaka" title="Maria Burmaka">Maria Burmaka</a> – Ukrainian singer, musician and songwriter</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Leonid_Buryak" title="Leonid Buryak">Leonid Buryak</a> - football coach and former Olympic bronze-medal-winning player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Leonid_Bykov" title="Leonid Bykov">Leonid Bykov</a> – Soviet actor, film director, and script writer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Adolphe_Mouron_Cassandre" class="mw-redirect" title="Adolphe Mouron Cassandre">Adolphe Mouron Cassandre</a> — Ukrainian-French painter, commercial poster artist, and <a href="/wiki/Typeface" title="Typeface">typeface</a> designer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Valentina_Chepiga" title="Valentina Chepiga">Valentina Chepiga</a> – <a href="/wiki/Female_bodybuilding" title="Female bodybuilding">female bodybuilder</a> and 2000 <a href="/wiki/Ms._Olympia" title="Ms. Olympia">Ms. Olympia</a> champion</li>

<p>The city of Kharkiv is one of the largest transportation centers in Ukraine, which is connected to numerous cities of the world by air, rail and road traffic. The city has many transportation methods, including: public transport, taxis, railways, and air traffic. There are about 250&#160;thousand cars in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">[187]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Local_transport">Local transport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Local transport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Being an important transportation centre of Ukraine, many different means of transportation are available in Kharkiv. <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_Metro" title="Kharkiv Metro">Kharkiv's Metro</a> is the city's rapid transit system operating since 1975. It includes three different lines with 30&#160;stations in total.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">[188]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PPoPmK_190-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PPoPmK-190">[189]</a></sup> The Kharkiv buses carry about 12&#160;million passengers annually.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> Trolleybuses, trams (which celebrated its 100 years of service in 2006), and <i><a href="/wiki/Marshrutka" title="Marshrutka">marshrutkas</a></i> (private minibuses) are also important means of transportation in the city.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Railways">Railways</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Railways">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The first railway connection of Kharkiv was opened in 1869. The first train to arrive in Kharkiv came from the north on 22 May 1869, and on 6 June 1869, traffic was opened on the Kursk–Kharkiv–Azov line. Kharkiv's passenger railway station was reconstructed and expanded in 1901, to be later destroyed in the <a href="/wiki/Second_World_War" class="mw-redirect" title="Second World War">Second World War</a>. A new <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_railway_station" title="Kharkiv railway station">Kharkiv railway station</a> was built in 1952.<sup id="cite_ref-uz_191-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uz-191">[190]</a></sup></p>
<p>Kharkiv is connected with all main cities in Ukraine and abroad by regular railway trains. Regional trains known as <a href="/wiki/Elektrichka" title="Elektrichka">elektrichkas</a> connect Kharkiv with nearby towns and villages.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Air">Air</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Air">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kharkiv is served by <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_International_Airport" title="Kharkiv International Airport">Kharkiv International Airport</a> has been granted international status. Charter flights are also available. The former largest carrier of the Kharkiv Airport — Aeromost-Kharkiv — is not serving any regular destinations as of 2007<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>. The <a href="/wiki/Kharkiv_North_Airport" title="Kharkiv North Airport">Kharkiv North Airport</a> is a factory airfield and was a major production facility for <a href="/wiki/Antonov" title="Antonov">Antonov aircraft company</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Recreation">Recreation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Recreation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kharkiv contains numerous beautiful parks and gardens such as the Gor'ky park, Shevchenko park, Hydro park, Strelka park, Feldman ecopark, etc.</p>
<h3><span id="Gor'ky_park"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Gor.27ky_park">Gor'ky park</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Gor'ky park">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Gor'ky park is very popular place for recreation activities among the visitors and local people.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Shevchenko_park">Shevchenko park</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Shevchenko park">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Shevchenko park is situated in close proximity to the V.N. Karazin National University. It is also a very attractive place for recreation activities among the students, professors, locals and foreigners.</p>
<table style="background:transparent;margin-top:0.5em;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ecopark">Ecopark</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kharkiv&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Ecopark">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Ecopark is situated at circle highway around Kharkiv. It attracts the kids, parents, students, professors, locals and foreigners to make the recreation activities.</p>
<table style="background:transparent;margin-top:0.5em;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto">
